  static memo<Result, Args extends unknown[]>(task: (deps: Args) => Result, ...args: Args) {
    const ctx = this.current!
    const index = ctx.cursor

    ctx.cursor++
    if (ctx.registry === undefined) ctx.registry = []

    const fiber = ctx.registry[index] ?? (
      ctx.registry[index] = new $mol_wire_fiber(this, task, ctx.toString() + index, ...args)
    )
    fiber.put_args(args)

    return fiber.sync()
  }

—è –ø–æ–∫–∞ —Ç–∞–∫–æ–µ –ø—Ä–∏–¥—É–º–∞–ª:
–∫–∞–∫-—Ç–æ –≥—Ä–æ–º–æ–∑–¥–∫–æ
class Handler<V extends Object> {
  protected subs = new Map<keyof V, $mol_wire_pub_sub>()

  get(t: V, key: (string | symbol) & keyof V) {
    let sub = this.subs.get(key)
    if (! sub) {
      sub = new $mol_wire_pub_sub
      this.subs.set(key, sub)
    }

    sub.track_promote();
    const v = sub.track_on()
    sub.track_cut()
    sub.track_off(v)

    return t[key]
  }

  set(t: V, key: (string | symbol) & keyof V, value: any) {
    const sub = this.subs.get(key)
    if (t[key] !== value) sub?.emit()
    t[key] = value

    return true
  }
}
